2026-05-29 04:58:24.072 +00:00 [INF] Executed DbCommand (6ms) [Parameters=[@userId='?' (DbType = Int32), @p2='?' (DbType = Int32), @p='?' (DbType = Int32)], CommandType='"Text"', CommandTimeout='30']
SELECT r1."Id", r1."UserId", r1.c, r1."CreatedAt", r1."UpdatedAt", s.id, s."itemId", s."itemName", s."quantityRequested", s."quantityIssued", s.status, s."Id0"
FROM (
    SELECT r."Id", r."UserId", CASE r."Status"
        WHEN 0 THEN 'PendingWithIssuer'
        WHEN 1 THEN 'Pending'
        WHEN 2 THEN 'Approved'
        WHEN 3 THEN 'Rejected'
        WHEN 4 THEN 'PendingAdminApproval'
        WHEN 5 THEN 'Received'
        WHEN 6 THEN 'NotIssued'
        ELSE r."Status"::text
    END AS c, r."CreatedAt", r."UpdatedAt"
    FROM "Requests" AS r
    WHERE r."UserId" = @userId
    ORDER BY r."CreatedAt" DESC
    LIMIT @p2 OFFSET @p
) AS r1
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT r0."Id" AS id, r0."ItemId" AS "itemId", i."Name" AS "itemName", r0."QuantityRequested" AS "quantityRequested", r0."QuantityIssued" AS "quantityIssued", CASE r0."Status"
        WHEN 0 THEN 'PendingWithIssuer'
        WHEN 1 THEN 'NotIssued'
        WHEN 2 THEN 'PendingAdminApproval'
        WHEN 3 THEN 'Approved'
        WHEN 4 THEN 'Rejected'
        ELSE r0."Status"::text
    END AS status, i."Id" AS "Id0", r0."RequestId"
    FROM "RequestItems" AS r0
    INNER JOIN "Items" AS i ON r0."ItemId" = i."Id"
) AS s ON r1."Id" = s."RequestId"
ORDER BY r1."CreatedAt" DESC, r1."Id", s.id

    WHEN 6 THEN 'NotIssued'
    ELSE r1."Status"::text
END, r1."CreatedAt", r1."UpdatedAt", u."Id", s.id, s."itemId", s."itemName", s."quantityRequested", s."quantityIssued", s.status, s."Id0"
FROM (
    SELECT r."Id", r."CreatedAt", r."Status", r."UpdatedAt", r."UserId"
    FROM "Requests" AS r
    WHERE EXISTS (
        SELECT 1
        FROM "RequestItems" AS r0
        WHERE r."Id" = r0."RequestId" AND r0."Status" = 2)
    ORDER BY r."CreatedAt" DESC
    LIMIT @p1 OFFSET @p
) AS r1
INNER JOIN "Users" AS u ON r1."UserId" = u."Id"
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT r2."Id" AS id, r2."ItemId" AS "itemId", i."Name" AS "itemName", r2."QuantityRequested" AS "quantityRequested", r2."QuantityIssued" AS "quantityIssued", CASE r2."Status"
        WHEN 0 THEN 'PendingWithIssuer'
        WHEN 1 THEN 'NotIssued'
        WHEN 2 THEN 'PendingAdminApproval'
        WHEN 3 THEN 'Approved'
        WHEN 4 THEN 'Rejected'
        ELSE r2."Status"::text
    END AS status, i."Id" AS "Id0", r2."RequestId"
    FROM "RequestItems" AS r2
    INNER JOIN "Items" AS i ON r2."ItemId" = i."Id"
    WHERE r2."Status" = 2
) AS s ON r1."Id" = s."RequestId"
ORDER BY r1."CreatedAt" DESC, r1."Id", u."Id", s.id

SELECT r1."Id", r1."Username", r1."Email", r0."Name" AS "Role", r1."RoleId", r1."Designation", d."Name" AS "Department", r1."DepartmentId", CASE r1."Status"
    WHEN 0 THEN 'Pending'
    WHEN 1 THEN 'Approved'
    WHEN 2 THEN 'Rejected'
    ELSE r1."Status"::text
END AS "Status", r1."CreatedAt"
FROM (
    SELECT r."Id", r."CreatedAt", r."DepartmentId", r."Designation", r."Email", r."RoleId", r."Status", r."Username"
    FROM "RegistrationRequests" AS r
    WHERE r."Status" = 0
    ORDER BY r."CreatedAt" DESC, r."Id" DESC
    LIMIT @p
) AS r1
INNER JOIN "Roles" AS r0 ON r1."RoleId" = r0."Id"
INNER JOIN "Departments" AS d ON r1."DepartmentId" = d."Id"
ORDER BY r1."CreatedAt" DESC, r1."Id" DESC

    WHEN 0 THEN 'Pending'

END AS "Status", r1."CreatedAt"

SELECT r1."Id", r1."UserId", r1.c, r1."CreatedAt", r1."UpdatedAt", s.id, s."itemId", s."itemName", s."quantityRequested", s."quantityIssued", s.status, s."Id0"
FROM (
    SELECT r."Id", r."UserId", CASE r."Status"
        WHEN 0 THEN 'PendingWithIssuer'
        WHEN 1 THEN 'Pending'
        WHEN 2 THEN 'Approved'
        WHEN 3 THEN 'Rejected'
        WHEN 4 THEN 'PendingAdminApproval'
        WHEN 5 THEN 'Received'
        WHEN 6 THEN 'NotIssued'
        ELSE r."Status"::text
    END AS c, r."CreatedAt", r."UpdatedAt"
    FROM "Requests" AS r
    WHERE r."UserId" = @userId
    ORDER BY r."CreatedAt" DESC
    LIMIT @p2 OFFSET @p
) AS r1
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT r0."Id" AS id, r0."ItemId" AS "itemId", i."Name" AS "itemName", r0."QuantityRequested" AS "quantityRequested", r0."QuantityIssued" AS "quantityIssued", CASE r0."Status"
        WHEN 0 THEN 'PendingWithIssuer'
        WHEN 1 THEN 'NotIssued'
        WHEN 2 THEN 'PendingAdminApproval'
        WHEN 3 THEN 'Approved'
        WHEN 4 THEN 'Rejected'
        ELSE r0."Status"::text
    END AS status, i."Id" AS "Id0", r0."RequestId"
    FROM "RequestItems" AS r0
    INNER JOIN "Items" AS i ON r0."ItemId" = i."Id"
) AS s ON r1."Id" = s."RequestId"
ORDER BY r1."CreatedAt" DESC, r1."Id", s.id

SELECT r1."Id", r1."UserId", u."Username", u."Email", CASE r1."Status"
    WHEN 0 THEN 'PendingWithIssuer'
    WHEN 1 THEN 'Pending'
    WHEN 2 THEN 'Approved'
    WHEN 3 THEN 'Rejected'
    WHEN 4 THEN 'PendingAdminApproval'
    WHEN 5 THEN 'Received'
    WHEN 6 THEN 'NotIssued'
    ELSE r1."Status"::text
END, r1."CreatedAt", r1."UpdatedAt", u."Id", s.id, s."itemId", s."itemName", s."quantityRequested", s."quantityIssued", s.status, s."Id0"
FROM (
    SELECT r."Id", r."CreatedAt", r."Status", r."UpdatedAt", r."UserId"
    FROM "Requests" AS r
    WHERE EXISTS (
        SELECT 1
        FROM "RequestItems" AS r0
        WHERE r."Id" = r0."RequestId" AND r0."Status" = 0)
    ORDER BY r."CreatedAt" DESC
    LIMIT @p1 OFFSET @p
) AS r1
INNER JOIN "Users" AS u ON r1."UserId" = u."Id"

    SELECT r2."Id" AS id, r2."ItemId" AS "itemId", i."Name" AS "itemName", r2."QuantityRequested" AS "quantityRequested", r2."QuantityIssued" AS "quantityIssued", CASE r2."Status"

        WHEN 4 THEN 'Rejected'
        ELSE r2."Status"::text

    FROM "RequestItems" AS r2

    WHERE r2."Status" = 0
) AS s ON r1."Id" = s."RequestId"

SELECT r1."Id", r1."UserId", u."Username", u."Email", CASE r1."Status"
    WHEN 0 THEN 'PendingWithIssuer'
    WHEN 1 THEN 'Pending'
    WHEN 2 THEN 'Approved'
    WHEN 3 THEN 'Rejected'
    WHEN 4 THEN 'PendingAdminApproval'
    WHEN 5 THEN 'Received'
    WHEN 6 THEN 'NotIssued'
    ELSE r1."Status"::text
END, r1."CreatedAt", r1."UpdatedAt", u."Id", s.id, s."itemId", s."itemName", s."quantityRequested", s."quantityIssued", s.status, s."Id0"
FROM (
    SELECT r."Id", r."CreatedAt", r."Status", r."UpdatedAt", r."UserId"
    FROM "Requests" AS r
    WHERE EXISTS (
        SELECT 1
        FROM "RequestItems" AS r0
        WHERE r."Id" = r0."RequestId" AND r0."Status" = 2)
    ORDER BY r."CreatedAt" DESC
    LIMIT @p1 OFFSET @p
) AS r1
INNER JOIN "Users" AS u ON r1."UserId" = u."Id"
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT r2."Id" AS id, r2."ItemId" AS "itemId", i."Name" AS "itemName", r2."QuantityRequested" AS "quantityRequested", r2."QuantityIssued" AS "quantityIssued", CASE r2."Status"
        WHEN 0 THEN 'PendingWithIssuer'
        WHEN 1 THEN 'NotIssued'
        WHEN 2 THEN 'PendingAdminApproval'
        WHEN 3 THEN 'Approved'
        WHEN 4 THEN 'Rejected'
        ELSE r2."Status"::text
    END AS status, i."Id" AS "Id0", r2."RequestId"
    FROM "RequestItems" AS r2
    INNER JOIN "Items" AS i ON r2."ItemId" = i."Id"
    WHERE r2."Status" = 2
) AS s ON r1."Id" = s."RequestId"
ORDER BY r1."CreatedAt" DESC, r1."Id", u."Id", s.id

    WHEN i0."Id" IS NOT NULL THEN i0."AvailableQuantity"
    ELSE 0

2026-05-29 11:51:19.015 +00:00 [INF] Executed DbCommand (39ms) [Parameters=[@p='?' (DbType = Int32)], CommandType='"Text"', CommandTimeout='30']
SELECT r1."Id", r1."Username", r1."Email", r0."Name" AS "Role", r1."RoleId", r1."Designation", d."Name" AS "Department", r1."DepartmentId", CASE r1."Status"
    WHEN 0 THEN 'Pending'
    WHEN 1 THEN 'Approved'
    WHEN 2 THEN 'Rejected'
    ELSE r1."Status"::text
END AS "Status", r1."CreatedAt"
FROM (
    SELECT r."Id", r."CreatedAt", r."DepartmentId", r."Designation", r."Email", r."RoleId", r."Status", r."Username"
    FROM "RegistrationRequests" AS r
    WHERE r."Status" = 0
    ORDER BY r."CreatedAt" DESC, r."Id" DESC
    LIMIT @p
) AS r1
INNER JOIN "Roles" AS r0 ON r1."RoleId" = r0."Id"
INNER JOIN "Departments" AS d ON r1."DepartmentId" = d."Id"
ORDER BY r1."CreatedAt" DESC, r1."Id" DESC
